  import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  import { NavigationProvider } from &#039;./contexts/NavigationProvider&#039;;
  import HomePage from &#039;./pages/HomePage/HomePage&#039;;
  import MoviesPage from &#039;./pages/MoviesPage/MoviesPage&#039;;
  import MovieDetailsPage from &#039;./pages/MovieDetailsPage/MovieDetailsPage&#039;;
  import NotFoundPage from &#039;./pages/NotFoundPage/NotFoundPage&#039;;
  import Navigation from &#039;./components/Navigation/Navigation&#039;;
  
  function App() {
    return (
      &lt;Router&gt;
        &lt;NavigationProvider&gt;
          &lt;Navigation /&gt;
          &lt;Routes&gt;
            &lt;Route path=&quot;/&quot; element={&lt;HomePage /&gt;} /&gt;
            &lt;Route path=&quot;/movies&quot; element={&lt;MoviesPage /&gt;} /&gt;
            &lt;Route path=&quot;/movies/:movieId/*&quot; element={&lt;MovieDetailsPage /&gt;} /&gt;
            &lt;Route path=&quot;*&quot; element={&lt;NotFoundPage /&gt;} /&gt;
          &lt;/Routes&gt;
        &lt;/NavigationProvider&gt;
      &lt;/Router&gt;
    );
  }
  
  export default App;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/components/MovieCard/MovieCard.jsx:
  import PropTypes from &#039;prop-types&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./MovieCard.module.css&#039;;
  
  function MovieCard({ movie }) {
    const imageUrl = `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`;
  
    return (
      &lt;div className={styles.card}&gt;
        &lt;img src={imageUrl} alt={movie.title} className={styles.image} /&gt;
        &lt;h3 className={styles.title}&gt;{movie.title}&lt;/h3&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
  }
  
  MovieCard.propTypes = {
    movie: PropTypes.shape({
      poster_path: PropTypes.string,
      title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    }).isRequired,
  };
  
  export default MovieCard;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/components/MovieCast/MovieCast.jsx:
  import { useParams } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  import { useState, useEffect } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import axios from &#039;axios&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./MovieCast.module.css&#039;;
  
  function MovieCast() {
    const { movieId } = useParams();
    const [cast, setCast] = useState([]);
  
    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      const fetchCast = async () =&gt; {
        try {
          const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}/credits?api_key=9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3`);
          setCast(response.data.cast);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(&#039;Error fetching cast:&#039;, error);
        }
      };
  
      fetchCast();
    }, [movieId]);
  
    return (
      &lt;div className={styles.cast}&gt;
        &lt;h2&gt;Cast&lt;/h2&gt;
        &lt;ul className={styles.list}&gt;
          {cast.map((actor) =&gt; (
            &lt;li key={actor.id} className={styles.item}&gt;
            &lt;img
              src={`https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w200${actor.profile_path}`}
              alt={actor.name}
              className={styles.actorImage}
            /&gt;
            &lt;p className={styles.name}&gt;{actor.name}&lt;/p&gt;
            &lt;p className={styles.character}&gt;as {actor.character}&lt;/p&gt;
          &lt;/li&gt;
          
          ))}
        &lt;/ul&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
  }
  
  export default MovieCast;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/components/MovieList/MovieList.jsx:
  import PropTypes from &#039;prop-types&#039;;
  import { Link, useLocation } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;; 
  import styles from &#039;./MovieList.module.css&#039;;
  
  function MovieList({ movies }) {
    const location = useLocation(); 
  
    return (
      &lt;ul className={styles.list}&gt;
        {movies.map((movie) =&gt; (
          &lt;li key={movie.id} className={styles.item}&gt;
            &lt;Link to={`/movies/${movie.id}`} state={{ from: location }}&gt;
              &lt;img
                src={`https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`}
                alt={movie.title}
                className={styles.image}
              /&gt;
              &lt;p className={styles.title}&gt;{movie.title}&lt;/p&gt;
            &lt;/Link&gt;
          &lt;/li&gt;
        ))}
      &lt;/ul&gt;
    );
  }
  
  MovieList.propTypes = {
    movies: PropTypes.arrayOf(
      PropTypes.shape({
        id: PropTypes.number.isRequired,
        title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        poster_path: PropTypes.string,
      })
    ).isRequired,
  };
  
  export default MovieList;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/components/MovieReviews/MovieReviews.jsx:
  import { useParams } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  import { useState, useEffect } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import axios from &#039;axios&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./MovieReviews.module.css&#039;;
  
  function MovieReviews() {
    const { movieId } = useParams();
    const [reviews, setReviews] = useState([]);
  
    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      const fetchReviews = async () =&gt; {
        try {
          const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}/reviews`, {
            params: {
              api_key: &#039;9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3&#039;,
              language: &#039;en-US&#039;,
              page: 1
            }
          });
          setReviews(response.data.results);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(&#039;Error fetching movie reviews:&#039;, error);
        }
      };
  
      fetchReviews();
    }, [movieId]);
  
    if (!reviews.length) {
      return &lt;div&gt;No reviews found.&lt;/div&gt;;
    }
  
    return (
      &lt;div className={styles.reviews}&gt;
        {reviews.map((review) =&gt; (
          &lt;div key={review.id} className={styles.review}&gt;
            &lt;h4 className={styles.author}&gt;{review.author}&lt;/h4&gt;
            &lt;p className={styles.content}&gt;{review.content}&lt;/p&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        ))}
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
  }
  
  export default MovieReviews;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/components/SearchBar/SearchBar.jsx:
  import { useState } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import PropTypes from &#039;prop-types&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./SearchBar.module.css&#039;;
  
  function SearchBar({ onSubmit, initialValue = &#039;&#039; }) {
    const [query, setQuery] = useState(initialValue);
  
    const handleChange = (event) =&gt; {
      setQuery(event.target.value);
    };
  
    const handleSubmit = (event) =&gt; {
      event.preventDefault();
      if (query.trim()) {
        onSubmit(query);
      }
    };
  
    return (
      &lt;form className={styles.form} onSubmit={handleSubmit}&gt;
        &lt;input
          type=&quot;text&quot;
          className={styles.input}
          value={query}
          onChange={handleChange}
          placeholder=&quot;Search movies...&quot;
        /&gt;
        &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot; className={styles.button}&gt;
          Search
        &lt;/button&gt;
      &lt;/form&gt;
    );
  }
  
  SearchBar.propTypes = {
    onSubmit: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
    initialValue: PropTypes.string,
  };
  
  export default SearchBar;

  export const NavigationProvider = ({ children }) =&gt; {
    const [prevPath, setPrevPath] = useState(&#039;/&#039;);
  
    return (
      &lt;NavigationContext.Provider value={{ prevPath, setPrevPath }}&gt;
        {children}
      &lt;/NavigationContext.Provider&gt;
    );
  };

  };

  Існуючий код для файлу src/pages/HomePage/HomePage.jsx:
  import { useState, useEffect } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import axios from &#039;axios&#039;;
  import MovieList from &#039;../../components/MovieList/MovieList&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./HomePage.module.css&#039;;
  import useNavigation from &#039;../../contexts/useNavigation&#039;;
  
  function HomePage() {
    const [movies, setMovies] = useState([]);
    const { setPrevPath } = useNavigation();
  
    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      setPrevPath(&#039;/&#039;); // Зберігаємо поточний шлях
  
      const fetchMovies = async () =&gt; {
        try {
          const response = await axios.get(&#039;https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/popular&#039;, {
            params: {
              api_key: &#039;9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3&#039;,
              language: &#039;en-US&#039;,
              page: 1
            }
          });
          setMovies(response.data.results);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(&#039;Error fetching movies:&#039;, error);
        }
      };
  
      fetchMovies();
    }, [setPrevPath]);
  
    return (
      &lt;div className=&quot;mainContent&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div className={styles.container}&gt;
          &lt;h1 className={styles.title}&gt;Popular Movies&lt;/h1&gt;
          &lt;MovieList movies={movies} /&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
  }
  
  export default HomePage;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/pages/MovieDetailsPage/MovieDetailsPage.jsx:
  import { useParams, Link, useNavigate } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  import { useState, useEffect } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import axios from &#039;axios&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./MovieDetailsPage.module.css&#039;;
  import { Routes, Route } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  
  
  import MovieCast from &#039;../../components/MovieCast/MovieCast&#039;;
  import MovieReviews from &#039;../../components/MovieReviews/MovieReviews&#039;;
  import useNavigation from &#039;../../contexts/useNavigation&#039;;
  
  function MovieDetailsPage() {
    const { movieId } = useParams();
    const [movie, setMovie] = useState(null);
    const navigate = useNavigate();
    const { prevPath } = useNavigation();
  
  
    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      const fetchMovie = async () =&gt; {
        try {
          const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}?api_key=9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3`);
          setMovie(response.data);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(&#039;Error fetching movie details:&#039;, error);
        }
      };
  
      fetchMovie();
    }, [movieId]);
  
    const handleBackClick = () =&gt; {
      navigate(prevPath || &#039;/&#039;);
    };
  
    if (!movie) {
      return &lt;div&gt;Loading...&lt;/div&gt;;
    }
  
    const imageUrl = `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`;
  
    return (
      &lt;div className={styles.movieDetails}&gt;
        &lt;div className={styles.columns}&gt;
          &lt;div className={styles.leftColumn}&gt;
            &lt;div className={styles.leftTop}&gt;
              &lt;button onClick={handleBackClick}&gt;Back&lt;/button&gt;
              &lt;img src={imageUrl} alt={movie.title} className={styles.movieImage} /&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;div className={styles.additionalInfo}&gt;
              &lt;h3&gt;Additional Information&lt;/h3&gt;
              &lt;div className={styles.additionalLinks}&gt;
                &lt;Link to={`/movies/${movieId}/cast`}&gt;Cast&lt;/Link&gt;
                &lt;Link to={`/movies/${movieId}/reviews`}&gt;Reviews&lt;/Link&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;div className={styles.rightColumn}&gt;
            &lt;div className={styles.rightTop}&gt;
              &lt;h2&gt;{movie.title}&lt;/h2&gt;
              &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Release Date:&lt;/strong&gt; {movie.release_date}&lt;/p&gt;
              &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Rating:&lt;/strong&gt; {movie.vote_average}&lt;/p&gt;
              &lt;div className={styles.section}&gt;
                &lt;h3&gt;Overview&lt;/h3&gt;
                &lt;p className={styles.sectionContent}&gt;{movie.overview}&lt;/p&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
              &lt;div className={styles.section}&gt;
                &lt;h3&gt;Genres&lt;/h3&gt;
                &lt;ul className={styles.sectionContent}&gt;
                  {movie.genres.map(genre =&gt; (
                    &lt;li key={genre.id}&gt;{genre.name}&lt;/li&gt;
                  ))}
                &lt;/ul&gt;
              &lt;/div&gt;
            &lt;/div&gt;
          &lt;/div&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
       
        &lt;Routes&gt;
          &lt;Route path=&quot;cast&quot; element={&lt;MovieCast /&gt;} /&gt;
          &lt;Route path=&quot;reviews&quot; element={&lt;MovieReviews /&gt;} /&gt;
        &lt;/Routes&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
  }
  
  MovieDetailsPage.propTypes = {
    
  };
  
  export default MovieDetailsPage;

  Існуючий код для файлу src/pages/MoviesPage/MoviesPage.jsx:
  import { useState, useEffect } from &#039;react&#039;;
  import { useSearchParams } from &#039;react-router-dom&#039;;
  import axios from &#039;axios&#039;;
  import MovieList from &#039;../../components/MovieList/MovieList&#039;;
  import SearchBar from &#039;../../components/SearchBar/SearchBar&#039;;
  import styles from &#039;./MoviesPage.module.css&#039;;
  import useNavigation from &#039;../../contexts/useNavigation&#039;;
  
  function MoviesPage() {
    const [movies, setMovies] = useState([]);
    const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();
    const query = searchParams.get(&#039;query&#039;) || &#039;&#039;;
    const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState(query);
    const { setPrevPath } = useNavigation();
  
    useEffect(() =&gt; {
      if (!searchQuery) return;
  
      const fetchMovies = async () =&gt; {
        try {
          const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/search/movie`, {
            params: {
              api_key: &#039;9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3&#039;,
              language: &#039;en-US&#039;,
              query: searchQuery,
              page: 1,
              include_adult: false
            }
          });
          setMovies(response.data.results);
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(&#039;Error fetching movies:&#039;, error);
        }
      };
  
      fetchMovies();
    }, [searchQuery]);
  
    const handleSearch = (query) =&gt; {
      setSearchParams({ query });
      setSearchQuery(query);
      setPrevPath(`/movies?query=${query}`);
    };
  
    return (
      &lt;div className=&quot;mainContent&quot;&gt;
        &lt;div className={styles.container}&gt;
          &lt;SearchBar onSubmit={handleSearch} initialValue={searchQuery} /&gt;
          {movies.length &gt; 0 ? (
            &lt;MovieList movies={movies} /&gt;
          ) : (
            searchQuery &amp;&amp; &lt;p className=&quot;noMovies&quot;&gt;No movies found.&lt;/p&gt;
          )}
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    );
    
  }
  
  export default MoviesPage;

  App.jsx
    import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
        import { NavigationProvider } from './contexts/NavigationProvider';
        import HomePage from './pages/HomePage/HomePage';
        import MoviesPage from './pages/MoviesPage/MoviesPage';
        import MovieDetailsPage from './pages/MovieDetailsPage/MovieDetailsPage';
        import NotFoundPage from './pages/NotFoundPage/NotFoundPage';
        import Navigation from './components/Navigation/Navigation';
        
        function App() {
          return (
            <Router>
              <NavigationProvider>
                <Navigation />
                <Routes>
                  <Route path="/" element={<HomePage />} />
                  <Route path="/movies" element={<MoviesPage />} />
                  <Route path="/movies/:movieId/*" element={<MovieDetailsPage />} />
                  <Route path="*" element={<NotFoundPage />} />
                </Routes>
              </NavigationProvider>
            </Router>
          );
        }
        
        export default App;

        import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
                import styles from './MovieCard.module.css';
                
                function MovieCard({ movie }) {
                  const imageUrl = `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`;
                
                  return (
                    <div className={styles.card}>
                      <img src={imageUrl} alt={movie.title} className={styles.image} />
                      <h3 className={styles.title}>{movie.title}</h3>
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                
                MovieCard.propTypes = {
                  movie: PropTypes.shape({
                    poster_path: PropTypes.string,
                    title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
                  }).isRequired,
                };
                
                export default MovieCard;

    MovieCast/
      MovieCast.jsx
        import { useParams } from 'react-router-dom';
                import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
                import axios from 'axios';
                import styles from './MovieCast.module.css';
                
                function MovieCast() {
                  const { movieId } = useParams();
                  const [cast, setCast] = useState([]);
                
                  useEffect(() => {
                    const fetchCast = async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}/credits?api_key=9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3`);
                        setCast(response.data.cast);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error fetching cast:', error);
                      }
                    };
                
                    fetchCast();
                  }, [movieId]);
                
                  return (
                    <div className={styles.cast}>
                      <h2>Cast</h2>
                      <ul className={styles.list}>
                        {cast.map((actor) => (
                          <li key={actor.id} className={styles.item}>
                          <img
                            src={`https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w200${actor.profile_path}`}
                            alt={actor.name}
                            className={styles.actorImage}
                          />
                          <p className={styles.name}>{actor.name}</p>
                          <p className={styles.character}>as {actor.character}</p>
                        </li>
                        
                        ))}
                      </ul>
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                
                export default MovieCast;
      MovieCast.module.css
        .cast {
                  padding: 20px;

    MovieList/
      MovieList.jsx
        import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
                import { Link, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom'; 
                import styles from './MovieList.module.css';
                
                function MovieList({ movies }) {
                  const location = useLocation(); 
                
                  return (
                    <ul className={styles.list}>
                      {movies.map((movie) => (
                        <li key={movie.id} className={styles.item}>
                          <Link to={`/movies/${movie.id}`} state={{ from: location }}>
                            <img
                              src={`https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`}
                              alt={movie.title}
                              className={styles.image}
                            />
                            <p className={styles.title}>{movie.title}</p>
                          </Link>
                        </li>
                      ))}
                    </ul>
                  );
                }
                
                MovieList.propTypes = {
                  movies: PropTypes.arrayOf(
                    PropTypes.shape({
                      id: PropTypes.number.isRequired,
                      title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
                      poster_path: PropTypes.string,
                    })
                  ).isRequired,
                };
                
                export default MovieList;

    MovieReviews/
      MovieReviews.jsx
        import { useParams } from 'react-router-dom';
                import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
                import axios from 'axios';
                import styles from './MovieReviews.module.css';
                
                function MovieReviews() {
                  const { movieId } = useParams();
                  const [reviews, setReviews] = useState([]);
                
                  useEffect(() => {
                    const fetchReviews = async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}/reviews`, {
                          params: {
                            api_key: '9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3',
                            language: 'en-US',
                            page: 1
                          }
                        });
                        setReviews(response.data.results);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error fetching movie reviews:', error);
                      }
                    };
                
                    fetchReviews();
                  }, [movieId]);
                
                  if (!reviews.length) {
                    return <div>No reviews found.</div>;
                  }
                
                  return (
                    <div className={styles.reviews}>
                      {reviews.map((review) => (
                        <div key={review.id} className={styles.review}>
                          <h4 className={styles.author}>{review.author}</h4>
                          <p className={styles.content}>{review.content}</p>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                
                export default MovieReviews;
      MovieReviews.module.css
        .reviews {
                  padding: 20px;
                }
                
                .review {
                  margin-bottom: 20px;
                }
                
                .author {
                  margin: 0 0 10px;
                  font-size: 18px;
                  font-weight: bold;
                }
                
                .content {
                  margin: 0;
                  font-size: 16px;
                }

    SearchBar/
      SearchBar.jsx
        import { useState } from 'react';
                import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
                import styles from './SearchBar.module.css';
                
                function SearchBar({ onSubmit, initialValue = '' }) {
                  const [query, setQuery] = useState(initialValue);
                
                  const handleChange = (event) => {
                    setQuery(event.target.value);
                  };
                
                  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    if (query.trim()) {
                      onSubmit(query);
                    }
                  };
                
                  return (
                    <form className={styles.form} onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
                      <input
                        type="text"
                        className={styles.input}
                        value={query}
                        onChange={handleChange}
                        placeholder="Search movies..."
                      />
                      <button type="submit" className={styles.button}>
                        Search
                      </button>
                    </form>
                  );
                }
                
                SearchBar.propTypes = {
                  onSubmit: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
                  initialValue: PropTypes.string,
                };
                
                export default SearchBar;
      SearchBar.module.css
        .form {
                  display: flex;
                  justify-content: center;
                  margin: 20px;
                }
                
                .input {
                  width: 300px;
                  padding: 10px;
                  border: 1px solid #ccc;
                  border-radius: 5px;
                  margin-right: 10px;
                }
                
                .button {
                  padding: 10px 20px;
                  background-color: #f0f0f0;
                  color: #000;
                  border: 1px solid #ccc;
                  border-radius: 5px;
                  cursor: pointer;
                }
                
                .button:hover {
                  background-color: #e0e0e0;
                }

    NavigationProvider.jsx
      import { useState } from 'react';
            import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
            import NavigationContext from './NavigationContext';
            
            export const NavigationProvider = ({ children }) => {
              const [prevPath, setPrevPath] = useState('/');
            
              return (
                <NavigationContext.Provider value={{ prevPath, setPrevPath }}>
                  {children}
                </NavigationContext.Provider>
              );
            };
            
            NavigationProvider.propTypes = {
              children: PropTypes.node.isRequired,
            };
    useNavigation.js
      import { useContext } from 'react';
            import NavigationContext from './NavigationContext';
            
            const useNavigation = () => useContext(NavigationContext);
            
            export default useNavigation;

  main.jsx
    import React from 'react'
        import ReactDOM from 'react-dom/client'
        import App from './App.jsx'
        import './index.css'
        
        ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById('root')).render(
          <React.StrictMode>
            <App />
          </React.StrictMode>,
        )
  pages/
    HomePage/
      HomePage.jsx
        import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
                import axios from 'axios';
                import MovieList from '../../components/MovieList/MovieList';
                import styles from './HomePage.module.css';
                import useNavigation from '../../contexts/useNavigation';
                
                function HomePage() {
                  const [movies, setMovies] = useState([]);
                  const { setPrevPath } = useNavigation();
                
                  useEffect(() => {
                    setPrevPath('/'); // Зберігаємо поточний шлях
                
                    const fetchMovies = async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await axios.get('https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/popular', {
                          params: {
                            api_key: '9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3',
                            language: 'en-US',
                            page: 1
                          }
                        });
                        setMovies(response.data.results);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error fetching movies:', error);
                      }
                    };
                
                    fetchMovies();
                  }, [setPrevPath]);
                
                  return (
                    <div className="mainContent">
                      <div className={styles.container}>
                        <h1 className={styles.title}>Popular Movies</h1>
                        <MovieList movies={movies} />
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                
                export default HomePage;
      HomePage.module.css
        .container {
                  padding: 20px;
                  text-align: center;
                }
                
                .title {
                  margin: 0;
                  padding: 20px;
                  font-size: 24px;
                  color: #333;
                }
                
                @media (max-width: 768px) {
                  .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(1, 1fr);
                  }
                
                  .image {
                    width: 320px;
                    height: 420px;
                  }
                }
                
                @media (min-width: 769px) and (max-width: 1158px) {
                  .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(2, 1fr);
                  }
                  .image {
                    width: 360px;
                    height: 480px;
                  }
                }
                
                @media (min-width: 1159px) {
                  .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr);
                  }
                
                  .image {
                    width: 420px;
                    height: 560px;
                  }
                }
    MovieDetailsPage/
      MovieDetailsPage.jsx
        import { useParams, Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
                import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
                import axios from 'axios';
                import styles from './MovieDetailsPage.module.css';
                import { Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
                
                
                import MovieCast from '../../components/MovieCast/MovieCast';
                import MovieReviews from '../../components/MovieReviews/MovieReviews';
                import useNavigation from '../../contexts/useNavigation';
                
                function MovieDetailsPage() {
                  const { movieId } = useParams();
                  const [movie, setMovie] = useState(null);
                  const navigate = useNavigate();
                  const { prevPath } = useNavigation();
                
                
                  useEffect(() => {
                    const fetchMovie = async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/${movieId}?api_key=9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3`);
                        setMovie(response.data);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error fetching movie details:', error);
                      }
                    };
                
                    fetchMovie();
                  }, [movieId]);
                
                  const handleBackClick = () => {
                    navigate(prevPath || '/');
                  };
                
                  if (!movie) {
                    return <div>Loading...</div>;
                  }
                
                  const imageUrl = `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500${movie.poster_path}`;
                
                  return (
                    <div className={styles.movieDetails}>
                      <div className={styles.columns}>
                        <div className={styles.leftColumn}>
                          <div className={styles.leftTop}>
                            <button onClick={handleBackClick}>Back</button>
                            <img src={imageUrl} alt={movie.title} className={styles.movieImage} />
                          </div>
                          <div className={styles.additionalInfo}>
                            <h3>Additional Information</h3>
                            <div className={styles.additionalLinks}>
                              <Link to={`/movies/${movieId}/cast`}>Cast</Link>
                              <Link to={`/movies/${movieId}/reviews`}>Reviews</Link>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <div className={styles.rightColumn}>
                          <div className={styles.rightTop}>
                            <h2>{movie.title}</h2>
                            <p><strong>Release Date:</strong> {movie.release_date}</p>
                            <p><strong>Rating:</strong> {movie.vote_average}</p>
                            <div className={styles.section}>
                              <h3>Overview</h3>
                              <p className={styles.sectionContent}>{movie.overview}</p>
                            </div>
                            <div className={styles.section}>
                              <h3>Genres</h3>
                              <ul className={styles.sectionContent}>
                                {movie.genres.map(genre => (
                                  <li key={genre.id}>{genre.name}</li>
                                ))}
                              </ul>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                     
                      <Routes>
                        <Route path="cast" element={<MovieCast />} />
                        <Route path="reviews" element={<MovieReviews />} />
                      </Routes>
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                
                MovieDetailsPage.propTypes = {
                  
                };
                
                export default MovieDetailsPage;

    MoviesPage/
      MoviesPage.jsx
        import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
                import { useSearchParams } from 'react-router-dom';
                import axios from 'axios';
                import MovieList from '../../components/MovieList/MovieList';
                import SearchBar from '../../components/SearchBar/SearchBar';
                import styles from './MoviesPage.module.css';
                import useNavigation from '../../contexts/useNavigation';
                
                function MoviesPage() {
                  const [movies, setMovies] = useState([]);
                  const [searchParams, setSearchParams] = useSearchParams();
                  const query = searchParams.get('query') || '';
                  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState(query);
                  const { setPrevPath } = useNavigation();
                
                  useEffect(() => {
                    if (!searchQuery) return;
                
                    const fetchMovies = async () => {
                      try {
                        const response = await axios.get(`https://api.themoviedb.org/3/search/movie`, {
                          params: {
                            api_key: '9004b6bfed6168d78cc5bc3b7fe243c3',
                            language: 'en-US',
                            query: searchQuery,
                            page: 1,
                            include_adult: false
                          }
                        });
                        setMovies(response.data.results);
                      } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Error fetching movies:', error);
                      }
                    };
                
                    fetchMovies();
                  }, [searchQuery]);
                
                  const handleSearch = (query) => {
                    setSearchParams({ query });
                    setSearchQuery(query);
                    setPrevPath(`/movies?query=${query}`);
                  };
                
                  return (
                    <div className="mainContent">
                      <div className={styles.container}>
                        <SearchBar onSubmit={handleSearch} initialValue={searchQuery} />
                        {movies.length > 0 ? (
                          <MovieList movies={movies} />
                        ) : (
                          searchQuery && <p className="noMovies">No movies found.</p>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                  
                }
                
                export default MoviesPage;
      MoviesPage.module.css
        .container {
                  padding: 20px;
                  text-align: center;
                }
                
                .noMovies {
                  text-align: center;
                  width: 100%;
                }
                
                @media (max-width: 768px) {
                  .container .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(1, 1fr);
                  }
                }
                
                @media (min-width: 769px) and (max-width: 1158px) {
                  .container .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(2, 1fr);
                  }
                }
                
                @media (min-width: 1159px) {
                  .container .list {
                    grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr);
                  }
                }
